# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="08d57-103">Chaînes de chiffrement Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08d57-104">Microsoft 365 tire parti de plusieurs fournisseurs de certificats différents.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08d57-105">Ce qui suit décrit la liste complète des certificats racine Microsoft 365 connus que les clients peuvent rencontrer lors de l’accès à Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08d57-106">Pour plus d’informations sur les certificats que vous devrez peut-être installer dans votre propre infrastructure, voir Planifier les [certificats SSL tiers pour Microsoft 365.](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08d57-107">Les informations de certificat suivantes s’appliquent à toutes les instances cloud mondiales et nationales de Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08d57-108">Last updated: **16/10/2020**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08d57-108">Last updated: **10/16/2020**</span></span>
